Quantum Bits (Qubits): The Fundamental Building Blocks\nTraditional Bit: Either 0 OR 1\nQubit: Can be 0, 1, OR both simultaneously (Superposition)\n\nAnalogy: \n- Classical Bit = Light Switch (On or Off)\n- Qubit = Dimmer Switch (Can be any brightness between on and off)\n\nMathematical Representation:\n|ψ⟩ = α|0⟩ + β|1⟩\nWhere α and β are complex numbers, |α|² + |β|² = 1\n\n2.
